Publishers and Teachers can also publish their content to the store to distribute to the learners.\r\n\r\nQuiklrn Reader\r\nThe Quiklrn Reader supports multiple formats from various content providers and publishers. This addition of documents onto your book is what we call as pinning of Qpins.\r\n\r\nBookmark\r\nBookmark functionality in the Quiklrn Reader, allows the bookmarks to be named or tagged. Naming the bookmark helps to retrace the bookmark easily.\r\n\r\nHighlight\r\nYou can simply highlight important sections on any page of your book.
